HereвАЩs the **latest materially significant update check** for Cursor, Claude Code (especially around workвАСtrees/cloud agents), and OpenAI Codex вАФ **automation turnвАѓ#2** (TueвАѓJanвАѓ20вАѓ2026):

---

### рЯІ† **OpenAI Codex вАУ Major product evolution**

**Codex continues rolling out substantial enhancements** beyond the original launch:"  
вАҐ Recent updates include a **revamped Codex CLI** tuned for *agentic coding workflows*, with richer tool use, progress tracking (toвАСdo lists), and enhanced modes for approval and workspace access.  
вАҐ A **new Codex IDE extension** allows tight integration into VSвАѓCode (and forks like Cursor), enabling cloud task previews, contextвАСpreserving work, and smoother localвАСcloud handoffs.  
вАҐ **Cloud agent improvements** boost task container caching (median completion times slashed ~90вАѓ%) and dynamic environment setup, including internetвАСbased dependency installs.  
вАҐ Codex now supports **code review capabilities** that reason over entire codebases, post results directly to GitHub PRs, and enable explicit review commands like `@codex review`.  
вЗТ This set of upgrades вАФ CLI, IDE extension, cloud perf, and codeвАСreview вАФ qualifies as a **major evolution of the Codex platform**. оИАciteоИВturn0search1оИБ

---

### рЯЦ•пЄП **Cursor вАУ Agent integration & model support**

**CursorвАЩs agent infrastructure has seen meaningful updates:**  
вАҐ CursorвАЩs **agent harness now supports OpenAIвАЩs frontier coding model GPTвАС5.1вАСCodexвАСMax**, with better toolвАСcalling and shellвАСoriented workflows.  
вАҐ While not a core вАЬversion bumpвАЭ release announcement, this model support is a **significant functional improvement** that raises CursorвАЩs agent quality and reliability with stateвАСofвАСtheвАСart models.  
вЗТ This is a notable material change in support for a new underlying coding model. оИАciteоИВturn0search6оИБ

**WorkвАСtrees / MultiвАСagent workflows:**  
вАҐ Independent reports and summaries describe Cursor 2.0вАЩs multiвАСagent interface *using isolated workspaces (вАЬworkвАСtreesвАЭ) for parallel model execution*, though that appears to be part of the V2 platform rollout from lateвАѓ2025 rather than new in this period. оИАciteоИВturn0search14оИБ
